### Post by Sonic Reducer on 2007-10-30
no program i have tried in linux has burned cd's on a consistent basis (gnomebaker worked on 2 cd's, but that was a while ago)

i think the problem lies in how linux sees the drive, because i rebooted into XP without even looking inside the case (i mean literally, i have an acrylic case lol) and it burned the cd the first time with no problems.

how can i adjust the buffer sizes? both buffers in K3b dont even flinch from zero before it says burn failed

### Post by Jimmyfj on 2007-10-30
In K3B go to Settings/Configure K3B/Advanced. Tick the "Manual writing Buffer size" and increase the buffer size which is set to only 4 MB.

---

### Post by MrFSL on 2007-10-30
AH SONY!!! -- < Insert Rant Concerning Sony Optical Devices >

If it works well in Windows and you are having a particularly difficult time getting Linux apps (which all primarily use the same command line apps to do the burning) might I suggest using Nero?

[http://www.nero.com/enu/linux3.html](http://www.nero.com/enu/linux3.html)

Try it then perhaps buy it. I use GnomeBaker. I have my dear mother using Brasero. -- But I also have Nero installed on both machines for those difficult burns.
